So you can tell just by the 8 that it will be last. Let us go back to the 3\'s. Since they both have 3 in the first place value move to the second. In the second place value, they have a 5 and a 4. So 4 is LESS than 5. So the one with 4 goes first. The one with 5 goes second, and the one that has 8 goes last :)! This is called least to greatest. So you can tell just by the 8 that it will be last. Let us go back to the 3\'s. Since they both have 3 in the first place value move to the second. In the second place value, they have a 5 and a 4. So 4 is LESS than 5. So the one with 4 goes first. The one with 5 goes second, and the one that has 8 goes last :)! This is called least to greatest. Three plus two is equal to five, and two plus three is equal to five. When you had three filled in, you needed two more to get to five. When you had two filled in, you needed three more to get to five. Notice three plus two, two plus three. Same thing over here, four plus one is equal to five, one plus four is equal to five.</div></div></div></div><div><div class="_1stkml6"><a href="http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-nc-sa/3.0" class="_18oxdcqr" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Creative Commons Attribution/Non-Commercial/Share-Alike</a><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=A-ykhY_IoaU" class="_vbe249b" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Video on YouTube</a></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="content-library-content-footer-portal" class="_8rq4olx"></div><div data-test-id="content-library-footer" class="_2tg0818"><div class="_1fg02run"><div class="_aofg6p5"></div><div class="_10up5c7o"><a role="button" class="_1kkrg8oi" href="/math/early-math/cc-early-math-add-sub-basics/cc-early-math-making-5-9/e/making-five"><span class="_1alfwn7n">Up next: exercise</span></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></main></div></div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n    \n    \n        <script>__HEADERS__ = {"X-KA-is-e2e":"false","X-KA-is-phone":"false","X-KA-is-tablet":"false","X-KA-is-unsupported-browser":"false","X-KA-is-ios":"false","X-Fastly-Country":"GB","X-KA-Lang":"en","X-KA-Locale":"en","X-KA-Locale-Status":"","X-KA-Curriculum":"uk-nc","X-KA-has-any-permissions":"","X-KA-may-be-under13":"","X-KA-is-phantom":"","X-KA-Static-Version":"230209-0743-d79d8c6f4377","X-KA-Published-Content-Version":"3ff80b863f5f6b2bcfdc1336afbfa015ef586fcd"}</script>\n    \n    <script>\n        __PAGE_SETTINGS__ = {"title":"","fullTitle":"Making 5 (video) | Making small numbers | Khan Academy","showTitleNotification":false,"description":"Learn for free about math, art, computer programming, economics, physics, chemistry, biology, medicine, finance, history, and more.
